Tin Mines Temporarily Suspend Mining 68

(Special Correspondence from Nanyang, Xiao Hui)

Suspension Date Must Not Be Less Than Two Months

Miner Unemployment Has Become a Major Problem

The period of one month of rubber tapping suspension has just ended, and the news of tin mine suspension has risen again. Rubber and tin are two important factors that determine the prosperity and decline of Nanyang, and they are of great concern to those who are in the tin industry, as well as those who are concerned about labor issues and social security. Since various tin trading companies in Sydney, Australia, proposed a three-month suspension plan, people in the tin industry have been shocked and concerned, and those concerned about labor issues and social security have also regarded it as a major hidden concern. The sales of tin are the highest in the United States and Britain. Now the production of tin is increasing day by day, but the consumption of tin has not increased. As a result, the production volume has formed a surplus, and the price has plummeted. Malayan tin mining companies have recently used water trucks for mining, and the production of tin is increasing. The production volume in May was 10,074 tons, while the world's consumption of tin is only 10,000 tons per month. Therefore, the tin produced by various tin mines in Malaya every month is sufficient for the world's use. In addition, the unlimited production of Australia has caused the supply and demand to lose balance. The current stock of tin has reached more than 40,100 tons. Since the stock of tin cannot be sold and new tin is coming in continuously, the price of tin has fallen step by step from 420 pounds (the highest price) to 132 pounds, 10 shillings and 2 pence (the current lowest price). It is unprecedented. If the market conditions are like this, all tin operators are running around in panic, trying every possible means to seek a slight turnaround. This is the origin of the saying of suspending production to save high prices. On June 14, the Malayan Four State Mining Association held a special general meeting in Ipoh. All participants were famous miners in Malaya, about 60 in number. The meeting was chaired by Mr. Ridge, the chairman of the Mining Association. After a long discussion on whether suspending the production of tin could save the market price, it was decided that the suspension date should not be less than two months, and the Mining Association requested the government to stipulate that tin mining should work six days a week, that is, one day off per week. As for when the suspension date will start, because there is no certainty about how to arrange the workers after the suspension, the Mining Association plans to convene another meeting and will announce it as soon as a definite solution is obtained. From this point of view, the suspension of tin mines is inevitable. It is difficult to predict what the effect will be after the suspension, but the two major problems that need to be solved urgently at present are relieving unemployment and maintaining social order. The problem of unemployment has spread to countries all over the world. Since the price of rubber and tin has fallen in Nanyang, unemployment panic has filled the minds of people from all countries. In addition, if tin mines are suspended, how will the more than 100,000 miners be resettled? The local government is considering the issue of relieving unemployment. It is reported that two methods have been proposed. One is to send Chinese workers back to their country, but this is not a consistent policy of the Malay Federal Government. The second is to build roads. There is a certain plan within the Malay Federation every year to develop its road administration, which requires a lot of workers. The Malay government may take this opportunity to try to resettle a large number of workers to engage in road construction. In the future, the government and the miners will jointly maintain unemployment. It is not known whether Jin Dabu's Chinese businessmen's tin mining company will participate in the suspension, so the number of unemployed miners can be reduced. As for the issue of maintaining social order, due to the serious problem of unemployment, it is rumored that someone has requested the government to temporarily prohibit the entry of Chinese tin workers. It is not known whether this is true or not, but in order to prevent bandits, the police in Ipoh have implemented martial law, and patrol teams are dispatched to patrol the city's borders and important areas every night. The night entrance to the city is under strict surveillance, and the situation is generally serious.

European Federation Movement 69

And its Current Difficulties (Special Correspondent in Europe, Hua Lu) (1) Origin of the European Federation Movement Europe is the birthplace of nationalism. Since the end of the eighteenth century, the nationalist movement has been extremely popular. Each nation maintains its language, religion, and culture, and demands political independence. As a result, the entire European continent has been divided into scattered pieces. This situation became more pronounced after the European War. The European War led to the collapse of the Russian, German, and Austro-Hungarian empires, giving rise to many new countries. In 1914, Europe had only twenty-five independent countries; now, it has increased to thirty-five independent countries and free states. Except for the territory of the Soviet Union, the total area of Europe is only 5.506 million square kilometers, with a population of only 360 million. Its land area is only half the size of China, and its population is even smaller than China's, but it is divided into three dozen countries. Some of these countries are as small as only dozens of square kilometers, and some have populations as small as only thousands. The Vatican, which was established last year, has an area only slightly larger than the Shanghai British Concession's racecourse, and a population of only 140-odd people, but it is still considered an independent country. Although the nationalist movement has enabled many small and weak nations in Europe to gain political independence and freedom, it has also divided Europe into scattered pieces. Most countries are too small and lack defense capabilities. In fact, they inevitably become semi-protectorates of several major powers, which leads to the formation of alliances among several strong countries, affecting overall peace. In terms of economy, there are even more difficulties. All European countries feel a lack of industrial raw materials and commercial markets. What one country lacks is possessed by another, and what one country has in excess is lacking by another. Because countries impose tariffs on each other, heavy tariff barriers are set up between them. The result of the Treaty of Versailles was to add 20,000 kilometers of tariff boundaries to Europe, making the circulation of goods very difficult and hindering the sales of industrial products. If we compare Europe with the United States, the area and population of the United States are roughly the same as those of Europe, but American goods can be sold throughout the forty-eight states of the United States without paying a single tax. In contrast, in Europe, they must go through more than thirty tax barriers. Under such circumstances, how can European industry compete with the United States? Therefore, from an economic point of view, Europe must break down the thirty-odd national borders and merge the whole of Europe into one territory in order to protect the industrial market of the continent on the one hand and compete with other continents on the other. Furthermore, politically speaking, Europe is divided into scattered pieces, and each country is suspicious and exclusive of the other, making it impossible to achieve a balance of power. In the past century, Europe relied on a "balance of power" to maintain temporary peace. The so-called balance of power relied on alliance treaties to divide the many countries of Europe into two sides, A and B. If the combined strength of the countries belonging to side A was roughly equal to the combined strength of the countries belonging to side B, then a balance could be maintained temporarily. This policy continued until the beginning of the twentieth century. At that time, Europe maintained a balance of power in the confrontation between the Entente of Britain, France, and Russia and the alliance of Germany, Austria, and Italy. But after the Great War, this balance of power was completely shattered. The policy of military alliances has been generally rejected by people. Europe can no longer form an alliance situation. But what else can be relied upon to ensure peace in Europe? The Kellogg-Briand Pact, the Security Pact, and arbitration treaties are nothing more than empty words on paper. Without a relatively complete international organization, the major and small countries of Europe will inevitably continue to oppress and exclude each other. The only way is to reorganize the many scattered countries and form a political entity so that everyone can live in peace. This is the origin of the European Federation Movement. Therefore, the significance of the European Federation Movement in the political aspect is to seek to replace the old-style balance of power policy and alliance policy in diplomacy. In the economic aspect, it is to open up the industrial market of the European continent and eliminate the tax barriers between European countries in order to compete with other continents. This movement is not only supported by the reformist social democratic parties and general pacifists, but also by European large-scale business owners, financial capitalists, and free trade advocates. Especially in recent years, as European industry and finance have been increasingly threatened by American capitalism, the theory of European Federation, the theory of Pan-European Union, and the theory of a pan-European customs union have been even more loudly proclaimed. For example, the Pan-European Union founded by Coudenhove-Kalergi has been promoting the establishment (a conference was held in Berlin last month, attended by many celebrities from various countries). But in the past, the scope of activity was limited to public opinion and had not been formally proposed by the governments of various countries. It was not until September last year that French Foreign Minister Briand made a proposal for a European Federation in Geneva, and in May this year, the French government officially published a plan for a pan-European alliance that the European Federation Movement gradually moved from the ideal to reality. Although this grand plan is still just empty words on paper, or may forever become empty words on paper, it is at least a noteworthy issue in recent diplomacy. News

Zhang Guizhou's Army in a Desperate Situation in Southern Hunan 70

The Eighth Route Army Strictly Prevents Escape to Guangdong Guangzhou Correspondence After the vanguard units of the Eighth Route Army, the three divisions of Jiang Guangnai, Cai Tingkai, and Li Yangjing, arrived in Hengyang, Zhang Guizhou's army retreated south from Liling via Youxian. Gui's army, led by Huang Shaoxiong, also moved from Changning via Leiyang. At that time, the two brigades of Huang Renhuan and Mao Weishou, which had entered Hunan from Guangdong in the second batch, were afraid that the 10,000-strong enemy entrenched in Leiyang would attempt to encroach on the Guangdong border. Chen Jitang, the commander-in-chief of the Eighth Route Army, also considered the situation in southern Hunan to be serious and ordered the two brigades of Huang and Mao to cease their advance into Hunan. Furthermore, due to the emptiness of Shaoguan's defenses, the Yu Hanmou division stationed in Wuzhou was transferred to northern Guangdong to strengthen the defensive works at the key fortresses of Maozifeng and Lianhuagang outside Shaoguan city. The Shaoguan branch of the Central Bank, in order to prevent any eventuality, transported the cash and banknotes stored in the bank back to the Guangzhou headquarters for storage on the 26th. The Li Zhenqiu brigade of the Yu Hanmou division stationed in Wuzhou also gradually transferred to Shaoguan on the 27th to await orders. Because the war in southern Hunan was still raging on the 25th, until recently, Zhang Guizhou's army again moved south with all its forces in Youxian. According to an air reconnaissance report on the 27th, the two divisions of Jiang and Cai of the Eighth Route Army had engaged in fierce fighting with the enemy in the northwest of Leiyang on the 25th and were still in contact on the 26th. According to headquarters news, the enemy gathered on the east bank of the Xiang River to attack Hengyang was composed of three regiments of Zhang Fakui's army and Li Zongren's guard regiment. On the 25th, the group launched several assaults on Hengyang, suffering over a thousand casualties. The enemy at Songbai (approximately 80 miles southwest of Hengyang) and Jiangkoutang was in contact with the sentries of the Eighth Route Army's Jiang division in Hengzhou, but had not advanced and reportedly showed signs of retreating towards Changning. In the Youxian area, the four-route army of He Jian had occupied Anren, etc. Finally, news was received from the 63rd Division at the front that the enemy had gathered over 10,000 men on the 25th and 26th to encircle and attack our army. After our army counterattacked and fought a bloody battle for an entire day and night, the enemy was unsuccessful and fled towards Changning and Chenzhou at night. Chen Jitang, the commander-in-chief of the Eighth Route Army, immediately ordered the two brigades of Mao Weishou and Huang Renhuan, as well as the Chen Hanguang regiment of the guard, to strictly deploy defenses in the areas of Lechang, Pingshi, and Jiufeng in order to consolidate the Guangdong border, and also transferred the 59th Division, the Yu Hanmou division, from Shaoguan to Lechang for defense. It is now ascertained that Zhang Guizhou's army is retreating south in two groups. Huang Shaoxiong's group appears to be leaving Xintian via Chenzhou to attack Pingshi, while Zhang Fakui's group is taking the road from eastern Hunan to Jiangxi, with the intention of cutting into southern Jiangxi via Lianhua. Therefore, Guangdong is making very thorough border defenses. (June 29th)

Han-Japanese Residents' Road Construction Case Over the Border 71

Japanese Consul States No Intention of Encroaching on Sovereignty The Municipal Government Replies to the Japanese Consul Expressing Understanding Hankou Correspondence The Hankou Municipal Government sent a letter to the Japanese consul requesting that he stop the Japanese residents' group from building Yongqing Road over the border. The government also sent Health Bureau Director Li Boren to negotiate. On the first of this month, Japanese Consul Tanaka replied to the Municipal Government, officially stating that there was no intention of encroaching on Chinese territory and sovereignty and requesting understanding to allow the completion of the project. The Municipal Government has replied in the affirmative and has informed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for record and has also instructed the Public Security Bureau and the Public Works Bureau. The relevant documents are excerpted below. The Japanese Consul's Reply to the Municipal Government In regards to the matter of the local Japanese residents' group slightly repairing Yongqing Road, we have received your government's letter Zhi Zi No. 1602 detailing the circumstances. However, this road is the only road connecting the Japanese concession to the Japanese park, and many Japanese people travel on this road. Moreover, due to the current summer season, even more people are entering and leaving the park, and the road is severely damaged, causing inconvenience to traffic. Therefore, the residents' group is bearing the cost of slightly repairing the road for the convenience of general traffic. If it does not rain, it is expected that the project can be completed within three or four days. However, in order to protect the repair project, we request that the police force directly responsible for the road, namely the Sanyuanli Police Station of your country, provide protection. This is a temporary and emergency measure for the convenience of traffic between Japanese and Chinese people. Therefore, our side has no opinion regarding the ownership of the roadbed or the police power on the road, and there is no intention to engage in any major actions that would infringe on sovereignty. We trust that your country will fully understand this and kindly reply to this letter after reviewing it. The Municipal Government's Reply to the Japanese Consul We have received your letter regarding the repair of Yongqing Road, stating that it is a temporary and emergency measure for the convenience of traffic and that it does not involve the ownership of the roadbed or the police power on the road, and that there is no intention to engage in any major actions that would infringe on sovereignty. After reviewing it, our mayor fully understands. However, according to the regulations for the construction and repair of roads in this city, the Public Works Bureau must approve the project before construction can begin. Since the letter states that the project is minor and is expected to be completed within three or four days, we can make an exception and allow the repair. In addition to informing the Public Works Bureau for record, we hereby reply to this letter for your information. The Municipal Government's Letter to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Regarding Request for Record Regarding the matter of requesting a record, our government received a report from the Public Security Bureau, which was forwarded from the 13th Police Station, stating that at 10:00 AM on the 5th of this month, they received a telephone call from the Japanese patrol station stating that the Construction Bureau of the Consulate General of Japan intended to repair the section of the road from the railway to the Japanese park, namely Yongqing Road, and requested that the police officers be instructed to protect all the materials and workers. Yongqing Road is within the jurisdiction of the 13th Police Station. The dispatch of personnel by the Japanese Construction Bureau for repairs is an act of encroachment over the border. Should it be stopped? Please review and instruct. After investigation, this case involves land issues, and an investigation by the Finance Bureau revealed that Yongqing Road is a public road and is not connected to the Japanese concession. The dispatch of workers by the Japanese Construction Bureau for repairs is indeed an act of encroachment over the border. The Public Security Bureau was instructed to reply by telephone to stop the project. The Bureau subsequently reported that the Japanese patrol station claimed that the repair of Yongqing Road was being handled by our residents' group and that they would reply after notifying the residents' group. If the Chinese Construction Bureau wishes to repair the road, please contact the residents' group directly. Please conduct a serious negotiation to demonstrate prudence. Our government sternly rejected this and sent Health Bureau Director Li Boren to the Japanese Consulate General to negotiate in person, requesting that the patrol station be instructed to stop work immediately. We have now received a reply from the Japanese Consul stating that the repair of the road is for the convenience of traffic and that it does not involve the ownership of the roadbed, police power, or sovereignty, and requesting understanding. In addition to replying to the letter temporarily approving the repair and instructing the Public Works Bureau and the Public Security Bureau, we are sending a copy of the circumstances and the four official letters exchanged between our government and the Japanese Consulate General to your ministry for record. Order to the Public Works Bureau and the Public Security Bureau (1) Order to the Public Works Bureau Regarding the Case for Information Our Bureau previously received a report from the Public Security Bureau, which was forwarded from the 13th Police Station (same as the letter to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs). In addition to replying to the letter temporarily approving the repair and instructing the Public Security Bureau to inform the Ministry for record, we are sending a copy of the original three letters to your bureau for information. (2) Order to the Public Security Bureau Regarding the Case for Information Regarding the case of Japanese encroachment over the border for road repair, your bureau previously submitted a report detailing the circumstances and requesting instructions, which our bureau sternly rejected and sent Health Bureau Director Li Boren to negotiate in person, requesting that the patrol station be instructed to stop work immediately. We have now received a reply from the Japanese Consul stating that the repair of the road is for the convenience of traffic and that it does not involve the ownership of the roadbed, police power, or sovereignty, and requesting understanding. In addition to replying to the letter temporarily approving the repair and informing the Ministry for record, we hereby instruct your bureau for information. (July 1st) Japanese Sakakibara

Encroachment on Official and Private Land in Liaoning Province 72

Shenyang Correspondence Sakakibara, a Japanese national who leases and operates a farm near the North Tomb in Shenyang, has repeatedly encroached on land outside the farm's boundaries. Negotiations have occurred more than once, and each time Sakakibara has made excuses. A month ago, the Japanese national even demolished a branch line of the Beining Railway, arousing public anger among our people. Serious negotiations were conducted with him, but the case remains unresolved to this day. Recently, it has been discovered that the farm has encroached on official and private land in two instances. (1) A section of official land is located north of the Xin Kaihe Wooden Bridge in front of the North Tomb, on the west side of the road leading to the Beining Railway Station, and north of the road, bordering the rice paddies cultivated by Sakakibara's farm. Sakakibara has erected barbed wire along the east side of the road, 10 zhang and 5 chi in length from north to south, and 8 zhang and 3 chi in width from east to west. Inside the barbed wire, he has erected wooden signs stating that it is construction land for the Sakakibara Farm Office. The Shenyang Municipal Public Office has sent personnel to investigate and confirmed that Sakakibara has not submitted an application for construction to the office and that he is indeed encroaching on official land outside the farm's boundaries. The matter has been reported to the Liaoning Provincial Government and a letter has been sent to the Commissioner of Foreign Affairs Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to initiate negotiations with the Japanese Consulate. (2) Farmer Wang Danian of the Dabeibianmen outside Shenyang, at the Shenhai Road Market, reported in the fifteenth year of the Republic of China that he had registered 61 mu and 6 fen of land in the restricted wilderness of Zhaoling, located northwest of the Provincial Third Middle School of the North Tomb. He has a deed, with the eastern boundary being Xiang Zizhong's land, the western boundary being the road, the southern boundary being Li Shuzheng's land, and the northern boundary being the paddy fields cultivated by Sakakibara's farm. The two sides are separated by a natural ditch. Zhang Guobin, a surveyor of the Land Survey Bureau, measured and released the land multiple times, and the mu count and boundaries were clearly established. At that time, special care was taken regarding the boundary issue because it was adjacent to Sakakibara's leased land. Subsequently, the land was leased for vegetable cultivation for four years, and everything was peaceful. Last summer, Sakakibara suddenly claimed that Wang Danian had encroached on his land. Wang Danian refuted the claim with reason, and the Japanese national retreated due to the weakness of his argument. Recently, Sakakibara has suddenly sent people to Wang Danian to claim encroachment and threaten to remove the seedlings if he does not return the land. Wang Danian has now petitioned the government to negotiate based on reason to protect civilian property and national territory. (27th)

Transportation Along the Jiaoji Railway For several days, the Jiaoji Railway has been unable to maintain its original schedule due to the military situation in Jinan. Currently, the trains departing from Qingdao only reach Fangzi, and those departing from Jinan only stop at Zhangdian and above. However, in addition to the railway security team protecting the trains, police officers are dispatched along the entire line to patrol, so there is no change in the order along the entire Jiaoji Railway, and all passengers can travel safely.

The Situation of the Northeast Flour Industry 74

Harbin Correspondence Before the tenth year of the Republic of China, there were as many as 28 flour factories in Harbin, and their sales reached Pingjin, Zhilu, and North Manchuria. The flour made from wheat produced in North Manchuria was unparalleled in color, aroma, and taste. After the twelfth year of the Republic of China, due to the strike at the Harbin Exchange, the market price of wheat temporarily rose from more than one yuan to more than three yuan, and the price of flour followed suit. American flour took the opportunity to enter the market. Later, when the turmoil subsided, American flour had already occupied the Liaoning area, and local flour lost a portion of its sales. Since then, the sales of the flour industry have been declining and have not recovered in recent years. Recently, Japanese nationals have taken advantage of the implementation of the new Sino-Japanese tariff treaty, utilizing the mutual benefit of tariffs to guarantee convenient transportation, and have begun purchasing our raw materials and setting up factories to manufacture flour, which they then import back into our country. They also receive additional tariff exemptions and low freight rates from the Japanese government. As a result, Japanese flour is steadily entering the four northeastern provinces and competing with our local products at low prices. The flour industry in the three provinces has suffered another blow, and many businesses have closed one after another. The twelve businesses that are still operating are only those with relatively strong capital. These twelve businesses produce approximately 63-64 train cars of flour per day, and local sales are only 15-16 cars per day. The remainder is transported to various towns along the Eastern Railway. Faced with this crisis, the flour industry in the Northeast is aware that if they do not take immediate action to save the situation, they will all be doomed. Therefore, the Flour Mill Association of the Three Provinces has initiated a plan to unite as a whole for common development and to research new methods to improve manufacturing. On the one hand, they are requesting the provincial government to take measures to maintain the industry to avoid mutual destruction. Currently, 43 operating flour mills in the three provinces have unanimously joined the organization and will be organizing in Harbin in mid-July in order to pool their efforts and strive to save the industry. Local correspondence.

Jiading 75

A Fatal Accident on a Bicycle Ge Zongan, the 14-year-old son of Ge Yanan, a resident of the north street of Anting Town in the county, is currently studying in junior high school. Yesterday (the 3rd) at 3 PM, he was riding a bicycle back and forth on the cobblestone road at the station, enjoying himself. While riding along the Yangqiao River, he accidentally fell into the water. Because he could not swim, he immediately sank. A Shaoxing boat happened to pass by and saw him, and they managed to pull him up. Although his body was not cold, he had no breath. He was rushed to the village sanatorium for treatment, but it was impossible to save him, and he died. Opening of the Grain Price Stabilization Program This year's grain price stabilization program in Jiading will follow the old practice of purchasing and transporting Xian rice with accumulated grain funds and distributing it to various districts in three phases for sale at a price of twelve yuan per dan. The price is calculated in terms of Feng Hu. After the rice is sold, the funds will be turned over for storage, and losses and transportation costs will be used for regular expenses. After the districts receive the rice, they will distribute it according to the previously established charts, with the price set at 230 wen per jin. Only poor households are eligible to purchase the rice, and the number of people per household is determined by the number of poor households in each chart. The program is expected to be completed within one month if the weather is clear (if the rain stops and the rice is received).

Fengxian 76

The Capture of Kidnappers and Hostages Yang Xingsheng, the captain of the Zhuangxing Police Branch, led police last night to raid a residence in Xinggangtan, about five miles from the town. They captured three male and female kidnappers, including Su Guiying, and rescued five hostages, both adult and children, surnamed Zhang and Gu. It is said that they were kidnapped from Zhangpu Town, Kunshan. They are currently being interrogated. The Party Committee Schedules a Departure Overseas Jiang Wenhe, an executive member of the County Party Headquarters, has been commissioned by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs as a consular trainee and ordered to work at the Korean Consulate. He is scheduled to depart overseas next week.

Jinshan 77

Robberies Occurring Frequently In Jinshan, robberies have been occurring frequently recently. The following is a summary of the robberies that have occurred in the past ten days: (1) Daoist He Changgen's home in Qianjiawei, Nanshejiaotou, had just received a donation and was targeted by bandits. On the night of June 23, several armed bandits broke into the house and robbed it, injuring He Changgen in the head. Silver dollars, white rice, clothing, and other items worth approximately three to four hundred yuan were stolen. (2) Gan Dejin's home in Ganxiang, Nanlouwu, was also broken into by dozens of armed bandits on the night of the 25th. The family members were first tied up, and then a large-scale robbery was carried out, resulting in significant losses. Gan Dejin's elderly mother was initially beaten and forced to confess, and then her lower body was burned, causing serious injuries. After the robbery, they fired guns to show off their power and left. (3) Fei Boat arrived at Lu Lantian's home, also in Louwu, at dusk on the next day. More than ten bandits broke in and robbed the house. Approximately seven stone of unpolished rice and silver dollars and clothing were stolen. (4) On the night of the 29th, several bandit boats arrived at Xu Peiyun's home in Ganxiang, Changyan. Many bandits broke in and committed robbery, forbidding anyone from making a sound. All two stacks of white rice were stolen, along with silver dollars, clothing, and other items, resulting in a significant loss. (5) On the same night, two bandit boats arrived at the Yang family in Ganxiang, Nan Heziwei. Many bandits stole more than 30 stones of white rice, 200 silver dollars, clothing, and other items. (6) On the evening of the 30th, several bandits broke into the home of Sheng Huhu in Shanqinggang, Hexi. They immediately tied up the victim and beat him in the main hall. Unexpectedly, the main hall collapsed, causing serious injuries that may be life-threatening. All belongings were stripped away, resulting in a significant loss. It is reported that in addition to the Tai Bao Ashu gang, there are many other gangs of bandits in the county. Among the Tai Bao Ashu gang, Zhu Luo Amei, Pan Amu, Wang Ajiu (all from Liujiawei), Xu Aijin, Dai Kechang, Sheng Xuejin, Aye (all from Qianjiawei), Xi Daoming, Gu Along, Gu Abu (all from Kongjiawei), Zhang Amu, Zhu Guitang (all from Lijialangxia), Yan Shusheng (from Zhuanjiaowan), Lu Yaosheng (from Dianxiaqiao), and Tai Bao Ashu's two younger brothers are said to be the most fierce.

Songjiang 78

Suspects apprehended in Tianmashan robbery case. On the evening of the second, more than ten bandits armed with knives and flashlights suddenly broke into the home of Sheng Shicheng, a resident of Lingjiayan, Seventeenth Township, Tianmashan, and robbed 420 yuan in cash. They then went to the home of a clan brother in the same residence and stole clothes and other items before fleeing. The victim immediately reported the case to the 12th Substation in charge for investigation. Subsequently,

suspicious residents were investigated. At the home of Xu Kanghou (also known as A'ba), a former local security guard, pawn tickets, smoking paraphernalia, a police whistle, and a knife were found. Nine hemp sacks belonging to Xu were also found. At the home of Ni A'si at the Lianlin Temple, hemp sacks and other items were found, which were considered highly suspicious. Xu Kanghou, his sons A'wu and A'qi, and A'si, a total of four people, along with the items, were taken to the General Bureau and then transferred to the county government for interrogation. It is said that, amidst calls for price stabilization of rice, a rice industry meeting was held. The county government had previously sent a letter stating that the rice businesses in Songjiang City had abundant rice reserves. It specially summoned rice industry leaders to advise on price stabilization to maintain food supplies for the people. Representatives of the industry held a meeting yesterday to discuss and resolve that, since the price of mixed rice has been gradually increasing since the beginning of spring, our industry bears the responsibility of regulating the people's food supply and should make a slight contribution to alleviate the situation. The eastern section will be organized by Zhang Sheng-san to collect rice and distribute it to the poor. The western section will follow established precedents and raise funds to organize a low-priced rice distribution point to help the poor, with Zhang Zhi-shi and Ye Ying-chun as directors. Currently, the highest price for white rice should not exceed 21 yuan per stone, with medium and lower grades decreasing accordingly. This has been reported to the public office for approval. The Ninth District Chief dismissed. Xu Zongjun, the chief of the Ninth District of Songjiang County, was accused of protecting gambling and abusing his authority. Suzhou 79

Appeal case of a chauffeur charged with rape scheduled for judgment. Zhang Zhiming, a chauffeur employed by the Shanghai Special Municipality Finance Bureau, was found guilty of raping Zhou Xiufen, a seventeen-year-old girl, in a case heard by the Shanghai District Court. Zhang Zhiming was sentenced to three years and six months imprisonment for the crime of harming public morals. Zhang appealed to the High Court, retaining lawyer Pan Zhenya. The High Court's Third Criminal Division held repeated hearings without reaching a conclusion. Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, the High Court again subpoenaed Zhou Xiufen and the Shanghai District Court's bailiff who investigated the case to appear in court, and Zhang Zhiming, who was in custody, was brought in for trial. After a lengthy interrogation, the court declared the debate closed and scheduled the judgment for the morning of the eighth of this month. Chang Chong's tax inspection results in robbery of boatmen. A boatman, Lu Cai, hired a boat from Zhu Jifu to pass through the Wulong Bridge area in the county. Six or seven bandits dressed in miscellaneous clothing boarded the boat under the pretext of inspection and robbed a gold bracelet and three gold rings before fleeing towards Gezhuang. Lu Cai immediately reported this to the patrol chief Ma Junwu of the police station in charge, requesting that the police be ordered to pursue the bandits, but they managed to escape. More than 400 refugees arrive in Huangdai, outside Qimen. On the afternoon of the third, four to five hundred refugees from Hunan arrived in Huangdai Town outside Qimen. District Chief Gu Kun reported this to the county government, which ordered them to leave the area by a certain deadline. Petition to restrict the public from wearing Western clothing. The Suzhou National Products Silk Machinery Relief Association believes that the public is increasingly wearing Western clothing, at a time when national products are declining. It has submitted a petition to the county government, which will forward it to the provincial and national government's Ministry of Interior and Ministry of Industry and Commerce, requesting that, based on clothing regulations, the public's casual wear should be standardized to national gowns and jackets, and that the indiscriminate use of Western clothing should not be allowed. Regulations for rewards and punishments should be drafted and submitted to local officials and the public security bureau for strict implementation to save the crisis in industry and commerce. The association has also scheduled a large-scale publicity week in mid-August. Wounded soldiers cause disturbances at the Women's Relief Center. At the Women's Relief Center (formerly the Jiliang Center) at Sanliowan outside Changmen, yesterday (the fourth) at 2:00 PM, more than ten wounded soldiers broke into the center and caused disturbances, entering the rooms of the women in the center. The center's director, Yin, reported this to the military police investigation office, which sent a team to suppress the disturbance. Two of the ringleaders were apprehended and taken for questioning. It is reported that the two troublemaking wounded soldiers will be sent to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters for disposition that night. Meeting to suppress and stabilize rice prices convened. The county government convened a meeting of the Rice Price Suppression and Stabilization Committee yesterday (the fourth), which resolved: (1) Rice merchants throughout the county hold approximately 20,000 stones of rice, and shops hold more than 50,000 stones, totaling over 80,000 stones. The market sells approximately 1,500 to 1,600 stones daily. The county government will instruct the Suyu Rui Gu two halls to inform all rice merchants and shops that they are not allowed to sell rice outside the county within three months. If anyone is found to be smuggling rice out of the county, it will be confiscated and used for price stabilization. (2) The selling price is set at a maximum of 19 yuan for top-grade white rice, 18.6 yuan for second-grade white rice, 18.2 yuan for third-grade white rice, 16 yuan for small high-grade white rice, and a limit of 16.3 yuan for ordinary coarse rice. This will be implemented from the seventh. (3) All shops must use labels and indicate prices for the grades of rice sold, and must not sell inferior goods as superior goods. Violators will be fined three times the value of the goods. Forcible pawning of blankets ordered to be prevented and suppressed. The Wu County Pawn Industry Association has reported to the county government for relief that recently, groups of people resembling wounded soldiers have been coercively pawning old clothes and military blankets at exorbitant prices, causing disturbances. The military police have been trying to stop them, but without much success, making it impossible to operate and forcing them to temporarily suspend business. The county government forwarded the matter to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters for review. Yesterday (the fourth), an order was received from the county magistrate to strictly prevent and suppress such activities, and to report the handling situation for verification.

Wuxi 80

Violent winds and rain capsize stone boat. The weather has been sultry recently, with thunderstorms occurring almost every afternoon. Yesterday afternoon at around 6:00 PM, dark clouds suddenly gathered, and thunder rumbled, followed by torrential rain. Two stone boats in Taihu Lake capsized near Yuantouzhu. Fortunately, the boatmen were all good swimmers and did not become victims of the waves. Also, the main fuse in the power plant's switchboard outside Qishu Yan in the west gate was broken by an electrical surge, causing the city's lights to go out for about half an hour. The factory repaired it, and the lights were restored. Undutiful son sells property unsuccessfully, twisting his father and throwing him into the river. Li Quangen (41 years old), a resident outside the north gate of Wuxi, used to work in the mountain goods industry, but he squandered his income at will. Recently, he quit his job and spent his days wandering around. Yesterday morning, he secretly went home and forced his father, Li Jingsheng (62 years old), to sell the ancestral property that had already been pawned. Jingsheng refused, and Quangen became furious, grabbing his father and dragging him to a nearby bridge, where he threw him into the river to drown. Fortunately, Ling Shunqing, a police officer on duty at the fifth branch of the Public Security Bureau, saw this and intervened, taking them both to the bureau and transferring them to the Public Security Bureau in the afternoon. Qian Yaonian, the chief of the Third Section, held a court hearing. Because the case involved disobedience, he ordered it transferred to the county government for interrogation. Cured wounded soldiers discharged from the hospital and returned to their units. The county government and the wounded soldiers' hospital jointly received a telegram from Commander-in-Chief Chiang, stating that wounded soldiers in the hospital should abide by the rules and focus on recuperation. Once cured, they should follow the regulations and be discharged from the hospital and return to their units. Recently, some unscrupulous wounded officers and soldiers have dared to shrink back and refuse to be discharged from the hospital after being cured, which is inappropriate. Therefore, two rules have been established to be observed: (1) Wounded officers and soldiers who are cured but refuse to be managed and refuse to be discharged from the hospital and return to their units will be charged with desertion in the face of the enemy. (2) Military personnel managing wounded soldiers and hospital staff who are ineffective and fail to diligently perform their duties will be charged with abandoning their responsibilities. Magistrate Sun and Hospital Director Cai received the telegram and immediately arranged for the cured wounded soldiers to be transported to the front lines to return to their units.

Changzhou 81

Robbery in Xinfeng Street, Wuyi. The Hexingchang Jinji Grain Store and Chen Zuocheng's residence on the north section of Xinfeng Street outside the north gate of Wuyi were robbed at 2:00 AM on the second. At around 10:00 AM on the morning of the third, the victim Chen Zuocheng encountered one of the robbers at Yangqiao Bridge. He immediately apprehended him and handed him over to the police on duty for interrogation. The robber confessed that his name was Cui Liurang, a substitute worker on the station platform branch road, but denied any involvement in the robbery. Subsequently, many road workers requested the police station to bail him out. The police officer summoned Mu Jiren, an apprentice at Hexingchang, who identified him as having come to the store with another person to buy cigarettes and joss paper before the robbery, looking around suspiciously. Chen Yu, Chen Zuocheng's wife, also identified him as the robber who stole their property at the time. The police officer detained him and transferred him to the county court for interrogation on the fourth. Woodworkers strike in Wuyi. The woodworkers in Wuyi demanded a 20% wage increase from the foremen. After days of negotiation, the foremen only agreed to a 10% increase. The workers, believing that the price of rice was too high and it was difficult to make a living, insisted on a 20% increase and went on strike on the third.

Jiangyin 82

Miao Shouzhi escapes from the bandits' lair. Miao Shouzhi, a wealthy resident of Zhanwen Bridge in the eastern suburbs, was kidnapped by bandits on the 20th of last month. Afterwards, there was no progress in the case. Miao's wife, Xue, received a handwritten letter from Miao Shouzhi a few days ago, stating that he was safe and sound and needed 30,000 yuan for ransom. His wife was trying to arrange the ransom when it rained heavily two days ago. When the rain stopped, Miao was found in a pile of firewood at Sunjiayan at the foot of Xiangshan. When Miao returned home, his family asked him about the kidnapping, but Miao frequently shook his head and refused to disclose any details. Public Security Bureau mistakes local defense force for bandits while arresting a witch. Tao Zuen, director of the Second Branch of the Qingyang Public Security Bureau, led three police officers to the area bordering Qingcheng City in Wuxi and Wenlin Township in Jiangyin on the second to arrest three witches (commonly known as "incense readers"). Unexpectedly, the Qingcheng City defense force mistook them for bandits and surrounded Director Tao and his officers, detaining them and handing them over to the Wuxi County government on the third. After receiving a phone call from Qingyang, Jiangyin Magistrate Li planned to inquire about the situation before taking further action. Li Zonggang, the director of the Public Security Bureau, dispatched Inspector Wu Qian to Wuxi to investigate everything. Excessive rain will cause disaster. Since the beginning of summer, it has been raining almost every day for more than ten days. As a result, walls and houses have collapsed in the urban area. Telephone and telegraph poles have also been struck by lightning and damaged, requiring daily repairs by craftsmen. In rural areas, dikes and low-lying areas have been severely flooded, causing the river to rise several feet. Small ferries operating between Chengxi, Chengwu, and other areas have been obstructed. Because the dikes are in danger, if the weather does not clear up soon, not only will transportation be hindered, but also agriculture and various social problems will be affected.

Yangzhou 84

Lifesaving reed rent changed to eight jiao. The Lifesaving Bureau of Guahao relies on the Xin Zhou reed rent for lifesaving funds, but the previous rent of 1,000 cash was equivalent to one yuan in foreign currency. Now, the foreign currency price has risen to over 3,000, and 1,000 cash is only equivalent to three jiao and three fen, making it extremely difficult to fund the lifesaving efforts. It has specially submitted a request to County Magistrate Chen to order the Relief Institute to review methods of providing relief. Yesterday (the second), the institute submitted a reply to the county government to change the reed rent to foreign currency at eight jiao per mu. The county government has ordered the bureau to notify the islanders to comply.

Pinghu 87

Two more robbery cases in the east countryside. The families of Sheng You-tang, Sheng Gui-rong, and Sheng Fang-yu, farmers in Beixin Village, Xinmiao Town, are located close to each other. Around midnight on June 30, they were simultaneously robbed by about twenty bandits, who had four or five guns. Most of them spoke with local accents and from Jinshankou. They first knocked on the doors of You-tang and Gui-rong's homes. Fang-yu took the opportunity to escape and ran to the village chief, Ma Jun's, house to sound the alarm. The bandits fired several shots in the direction of the alarm, but missed. They then divided into groups and looted, showing no fear. They tied up and beat You-tang, Gui-rong, and Fang-yu's son, Jin-sheng, causing them serious injuries. The losses were greater for the You-tang and Gui-rong families. After the robbery, they blew a horn and gathered in the direction of Luwan Temple in the southeast before leaving. On the same night at around 1:00 AM, the home of Hu Jinrong near Ma Fulin in Xielefang was also robbed by more than ten bandits who broke down the door and looted for a long time before leaving in a southerly direction towards Xiuping Bridge. The victims in both villages reported the incidents to Xin-cang, requesting strict investigation and apprehension of the bandits. Xin-dai water police apprehend robber. Mao Yunsheng, an investigator from the third squad of the ninth team of the Xin-dai water police, apprehended the robber Shen Shaolan at the Xiyuan teahouse in the town on the 29th of last month. Shen is from Qujiaqiao, Xingta, Jinshan County, and works as a tailor. He was identified by Lu Lansheng, the victim in the Jiudai robbery case, as the main culprit in the case. It is reported that he was sent to the ninth team and then to the county government for legal action.

Hangzhou 88

Measures for land use for the Xiaochang Railway. After research, it has been decided that they should not be allowed to register and serve as members of the Chamber of Commerce.

Shangyu 89

District education officer expenses have become a problem. The county's school districts are divided according to the seven party districts of the former temporary party headquarters in the county, with one education officer per district receiving a monthly salary of 30 yuan. This salary is paid from the self-governance surcharge. Now that the district offices have been established, the provincial government previously ordered the county to return the 2,600 yuan in annual salaries of the district education officers by the end of May to be used for the district offices' expenses. After receiving the order, the education authorities found it difficult to raise the funds due to a severe shortage of education funds. It is absolutely impossible for the education administrative personnel, the district education officers, to be penny-pinching and starving themselves. This will affect the progress of education and hinder the development of school affairs. In addition to submitting the difficult situation to the province and requesting permission to continue paying the salaries as before, it was decided at the county education committee meeting a few days ago to temporarily borrow from the county government before receiving the provincial order. Graduation statistics for elementary schools. There are 218 primary schools, both higher and lower grades, in Shangyu County, with over 400 teachers and over 12,000 male and female students. According to the Education Bureau's statistics, from May 22 to the 2nd of this month, 15 county, district, and private complete elementary schools received senior-level graduation certificates, graduating 161 students.

Letter from Zhu Fang, Attorney 90

Dear Sir: I have been instructed by my uncle, Mr. Zhu Kongwen, that yesterday, upon returning to Shanghai from Suzhou, he saw a news item in the local section of your newspaper titled "Suspicious Actions, Investigation in Shanghai," which stated that Zhu Tingyu, Zhu Ronggui, Xiao Yunzhang, and others from Shanghai, claiming to be master and servants, were acting suspiciously and were detained and interrogated by the county government without providing any clear confessions. Zhu Tingyu also telegraphed Zhu Kongwen in Sanlintang, Pudong, requesting him to come and provide proof. He was greatly shocked to discover that there is no one named Zhu Tingyu or Zhu Ronggui in our family, nor is there anyone with such names among his friends. He also did not receive the telegram mentioned. It is feared that the information in your newspaper is based on hearsay. I have been instructed to request a correction. Zhu Fang, Attorney, July 4, 19th year.

Local Silver Reserves Decline Again 93

A decrease of 1,265,000 taels

As of yesterday, the local silver reserves have decreased significantly due to the lack of foreign silver imports and the large number of silver ingot exports. According to a survey, the current silver reserves are as follows: (1) Silver ingots and regulated silver: 110,028,000 taels, a decrease of 453,000 taels. (2) Silver dollars: 157,480,000 yuan, a decrease of 1,130,000 yuan. The above, converted to silver price, is 223,041,300 taels, a net decrease of 1,265,000 taels of silver.

Huge Amount of Silver Ingot Exports 94

Silver price is maintained

According to a survey, foreign banks in Shanghai have recently shipped a large batch of silver ingots for export to Bombay for sale. These include HSBC, Chase, McCallie, and Mercantile Bank, with a total export of approximately 2 million ounces of silver ingots. As a result, the local silver reserves have been reduced significantly, and the silver price has been maintained.

Japanese Ship Violently Collides with Chinese Warship 95

The Dali Maru is heavily damaged.

The Weisheng warship is also damaged.

The responsibility lies entirely with the Japanese ship.

The Dali Maru, a Yangtze River vessel belonging to the Nissin Company, was heading to Shanghai from Hankou and collided with a naval warship while docked in Huangshigang. Both sides were injured. The Dali Maru has returned to Shanghai. The details are as follows:

Collision circumstances. The Dali Maru departed from Hankou at 9:00 PM on July 1. Recently, night navigation has been allowed in the Huangzhou-Daye area, so the ship sailed as usual. At 4:30 AM (on the morning of the 2nd), the ship arrived in Huangshigang. The Chinese naval warship Weisheng was docked there. The warship was ordered to suppress bandits and escort ships, so it was anchored in the river. Unexpectedly, when the Dali Maru was passing by the Weisheng warship, the stern of the ship was forced sideways by the current and crashed into the warship's bow. The Weisheng was anchored and could not move. With a loud crash, the stern of the Dali Maru crashed into the bow of the warship.

Damage condition. The accident was entirely the fault of the Japanese ship for negligent navigation. After the collision, the Dali Maru quickly reversed and backed away, but the bow of the Weisheng warship was damaged, and the stern of the Dali Maru was also severely damaged. Due to the intense impact, the entire second floor of the stern was destroyed, and all the passenger seats, office rooms, etc., were completely collapsed. Fortunately, the crew and passengers escaped from the rooms and were not injured. Also, the outer hull of the stern was also damaged. Fortunately, it was above the waterline, so the ship was able to safely return to Shanghai.

Inspection and repairs in Shanghai. Yesterday, the ship arrived in Shanghai and docked at the Pudong Wharf. First, the cargo in each cabin was unloaded, and then the shipowner reported the incident to the company. The company has scheduled an engineer to inspect the ship today to determine the basis for repairs. The extent of damage to the head of the Weisheng warship must also be verified before negotiations can be conducted.

A Simple Explanation of the Cooperative Movement 96

(1) The cooperative movement is a new global economic organization movement intended to remedy the shortcomings of modern economic organizations that are solely profit-driven, by using cooperative organizations to connect producers and consumers, thereby eliminating the parasitic class of merchants who profit from the difference. This prevents producers from being manipulated and oppressed, and consumers from being exploited and controlled. It also aims to eliminate commercial warfare, prevent large enterprises from monopolizing, reconcile labor-capital conflicts, eliminate usury, and equalize economic profits through peaceful, thrifty, fair, self-reliant, and mutually supportive methods.

(2) The cooperative movement can unite the national spirit. The greatest defect of the Chinese nation is that it has always been a disunited mass. Therefore, to restore the inherent strength of the nation and promote lofty national consciousness, it is necessary to start with uniting the people. Engaging in cooperative enterprises can achieve the benefits of unity, and unconsciously cultivate a spirit of self-reliance, mutual assistance, shared virtues, shared hearts, shared joys, and shared sorrows, which is a great help to uniting the nation.

(3) The cooperative movement can promote the development of civil rights. The development of civil rights must start with training, hence the preliminary view of civil rights that "no gathering, no success." In a cooperative, "power" is in the hands of the members, while "ability" is the responsibility of specialists elected by the members. The "one person, one vote" system of cooperatives embodies the spirit of democracy, and its situation is the same as the separation of powers in the country. Therefore, the practice of working within cooperatives can provide training for the exercise of the four rights of election, recall, initiative, and referendum, and is a good method for promoting the realization of the principle of civil rights.

(4) The cooperative movement is the first step in realizing the Principle of People's Livelihood. The purpose of the cooperative movement is to achieve self-sufficiency for the people, not profit-making like capitalism, and to build a consciously economic organization that is equal, fair, and nurtures the people with a definite plan. Its purpose is the same as the Principle of People's Livelihood. However, the Principle of People's Livelihood has the power of politics, which uses legal systems to suppress the manipulation of landlords and capitalists and protect the rights of farmers and laborers. The cooperative movement is purely the effort of the people themselves and is solely an organizational method in the economic aspect, which is slightly different. However, only in this way can the economic power of the people themselves, gained through the efforts of the cooperative movement, be a supplement to political power and promote the success of the Principle of People's Livelihood. Therefore, the cooperative movement is the first step in realizing the Principle of People's Livelihood, and the cooperative movement can only succeed under the promotion of the Principle of People's Livelihood. It is to make cooperation materialize the Principle of People's Livelihood, not to cooperate the Principle of People's Livelihood.

(5) The cooperative movement is the foundation for establishing local autonomy. Local autonomy is the organization of local people managing their own politics and economy. The experience of cooperative enterprises can cultivate the concepts of self-help, self-reliance, and self-defense, which can also cultivate the foundation of autonomy. Therefore, the Premier has stipulated in the Local Autonomy Implementation Law that autonomous organs should promote cooperative enterprises. Now, in the midst of preparing for local autonomy, we should especially promote the cooperative movement to help each other forward.

(6) The cooperative movement can alleviate the suffering of farmers. Farmers account for more than 80% of the country's population. In addition to the difficulties in borrowing money, which affects their daily life hardships, the most painful thing is that the tiller cannot own his land. Therefore, in the Premier's equalization of land rights, in addition to formulating laws to restrict, protect, and reward, there are also provisions to support farmers in purchasing land so that they can "the tiller has his own land". The function of the cooperative is to use the spirit of connection and cooperation: (1) Apply consumer cooperatives so that farmers can directly purchase daily necessities from producers or wholesalers, avoiding the profits obtained by merchants through middlemen, and saving daily expenses. (2) Apply supply cooperatives so that farmers can jointly purchase fertilizers, seeds, and tools to increase the effectiveness of technology and increase the power of production. (3) Apply sales cooperatives so that farmers can sell directly to avoid merchants' exploitation and manipulation to increase the price of production. (4) Apply manufacturing cooperatives to enable farmers to jointly manufacture agricultural products that must be manufactured by machines, such as dairy products, to increase daily income. (5) Apply credit cooperatives to circulate assets, allowing farmers to improve their daily lives and obtain capital to purchase land, so that the tiller has his own land.

(7) The cooperative movement is the movement to liberate workers and small merchants. Because workers also suffer from the pain of lacking capital, even the lowest living standards are almost impossible to maintain. Therefore, the Premier's provisions for workers' relief include setting the highest and lowest wage limits, formulating factory management laws, determining labor insurance systems, and adopting profit-sharing systems to provide relief. However, all of these are legal provisions and equal assistance. If one can engage in the cooperative movement and strive for liberation on one's own, the results will surely be faster. Because production cooperatives can make workers the co-owners of factories, machines, and all production tools; construction cooperatives can make workers the co-owners of real estate; and consumer cooperatives can not only improve the daily lives of workers, but also make them shareholders and co-owners of savings in the society. Other urban small merchants also suffer from the pain of poor economic organization, no less than farmers and workers. Therefore, they can also organize cooperatives to avoid the oppression of large stores and reduce the cost of purchasing goods to generate more capital and improve their lives.

Slogans: (1) The cooperative movement is the first step in realizing the Principle of People's Livelihood. (2) The cooperative movement is the weapon to solve our country's economic problems. (3) The cooperative movement is the movement to develop the economy of the common people. (4) The cooperative movement can create capital. (5) The cooperative movement can regulate capital. (6) The cooperative movement can enable the tiller to have his own land. (7) The cooperative movement can establish the foundation of local autonomy. (8) The cooperative movement can eliminate social waste. (9) Cooperatives are the banks of the common people. (10) Cooperatives can eliminate the pain of usury. (11) Cooperatives can make prices low. (12) Cooperation can prevent the monopoly of large enterprises. (13) Cooperation can cultivate good morals. (14) Cooperation can cultivate thrifty habits. (15) Cooperation can improve the lives of farmers and workers. (16) Cooperation can promote the development of production. (17) Cooperation is "everyone for me, I for everyone." (18) The people of the whole country unite to participate in the cooperative movement.

Propaganda Department of the Shanghai Special City Party Department of the Chinese Kuomintang

Sales of Chinese Tea in Russia 97

Fierce Competition from Japanese Merchants

Serious Blow to Chinese Merchants

The annual sales of Chinese tea exported to Russia are quite large. Since the problem with Sino-Russian relations occurred, Sino-Russian trade has virtually stopped. Japanese merchants have taken the opportunity to compete fully, taking away most of the original position of Chinese tea in Russia. According to the statistics of the commercial officer of the Japanese embassy yesterday, Russian merchants have already placed orders with Japanese flower companies for this year (year 19), including Fuji Trading Co., Shizuoka Trading Co., etc., for about 4.2 million pounds. In addition, there are more than 100,000 pounds of orders from Russian merchants in Kyushu, Ureshino, and other places. It is found that in the past year, the largest number of Japanese tea exports to Russia was only 3.3 million pounds. It has suddenly increased by more than 1 million pounds in one year. These are all the original sales of Chinese tea that have been newly seized by Japanese tea. Therefore, the blow to Chinese tea is really shocking. Reported by the Japanese Embassy in China.

The French Concession Water and Electricity Workers' Strike 100

Hope for Resolution

Mediator has Agreed to Three Conditions

The Two Detained Workers Were Released Yesterday

Work Expected to Resume at 9:00 AM This Morning

The French Concession Water and Electricity Workers' strike was mediated yesterday by a mediator, and the union dispatched four representatives, including Xu Amei, to negotiate. The news from yesterday is recorded as follows:

Release of Workers: The two workers, Zhou Aliu and Liu Linsheng, who were previously detained by the French police, were bailed out by the mediator on the evening of the 2nd and handed over to the four representatives to be completely free. As for Song Youxing, who was detained by the Public Security Bureau, it has been agreed to release him last night.

Negotiation Process: The four union representatives originally planned that the factory should pay the wages for the strike period, and all workers should resume work first. It was agreed that the conditions would be resolved about 14 days ago. Later, the four representatives returned to the union to hold a plenary meeting. The workers unanimously requested the mediator to agree to the conditions before resuming work. At that time, Chen Jifan and Cui Guangyu were waiting for news at the union and immediately returned to the mediator to report the situation at the meeting.

Agreement to Three Conditions: After discussion, three conditions should be agreed to first: (1) Wages will be paid during the strike period. (2) Increase wages. (3) Solatium.

Passage of Resumption of Work: The two representatives returned to the meeting to report the three conditions that had been agreed to. Xu Amei then opened a meeting to discuss the matter, and it was unanimously agreed that the three conditions had been agreed to verbally and should be implemented on schedule. As for the remaining conditions, negotiations should continue after the resumption of work. The mediator's representative agreed to convey the message, asking all workers to rest assured and asking them to elect representatives to consult with the mediator again in order to resume work as soon as possible. The meeting then elected Xu Amei, Zheng Ruisheng, Chen Puai, Xu Yukun, and others to formally receive the conditions. It is still necessary to submit the report to the Municipal Party Committee and the Social Affairs Bureau for approval and to sign a treaty. If it is satisfactory, the resumption of work is expected to be realized at 9:00 AM this morning.

Low-Priced Rice Opens for Sale in Pu Song District 105

Municipal Commissioner Chen Yafu of Pu Song District, seeing that the poor residents of Pu Song were greatly affected by the high price of rice, specially obtained 400 bags of low-priced rice from the low-priced rice committee of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau. They were loaded at Pu Song the day before yesterday, priced at 15 yuan per stone and 450 yuan per liter, and started selling at low prices yesterday (July 4) from 8:00 am to 11:00 am and from 1:00 pm to 4:00 pm every day. One liter for a large family and half a liter for a small family. The low-priced rice selling point is located at the Municipal Commissioner's office. The staff is hired by the Municipal Commissioner's office and staff from various rice shops are jointly responsible for the handling. The method is that the head of each district first goes to investigate the extremely poor households and issues low-priced rice purchase certificates in order to benefit the poor and relieve their hardships. Yesterday was the first day of low-priced rice selling, and those who held tickets to buy rice were very enthusiastic.

Bread-Eating Campaign 106

Talk of an Economist

The recent price of rice has risen sharply, causing panic among the people. Yesterday, an economist talked about the bread problem as follows: The Shanghai proverb "thousands of pigs and ten thousand rice" describes the large population of the city. In fact, in recent years, the population has increased sharply, and ten thousand stones of rice cannot supply one day's food. The sound of panic over the people's food is rampant. To solve this problem, one must eat flour twice a week. Calculating with 3 million people, each person eats half a liter of rice per day, which requires 15,000 stones of rice. Eating flour for eight days for four weeks a month can reduce rice by 120,000 stones per month. If it can be implemented, the price of rice will be flat by itself. It is found that about 7 million stones of Saigon rice are purchased in the city, and at 15 yuan per stone, the money outflow will be more than 100 million yuan. If the leakage is not stopped, social and economic panic will be seen. According to the current flour price, No. 2 flour is 9 cents per catty. The current rice price is more than 1.5 cents per catty. Comparing eating rice with eating noodles, it is indeed a significant fact that economic savings are made. It is also found that there are many kinds of wheat, but wheat can be made into flour for various foods. All provinces in our country produce rice, but the Yangtze River Basin produces more. Therefore, the northern provinces have always been dominated by noodles, and the southern provinces have been dominated by rice. Now, when the price of rice is rising sharply, it is appropriate to change to eating flour. There are dozens of flour mills in the country, and there are 14 mills currently operating in Shanghai. The total flour produced in Shanghai every day is about 120,000 bags. Originally, each person needs to eat more than one liter of rice per day, but now each bag weighs 49 pounds and can replace a lot of rice. Recently, it was heard that Fuxin and other factories have already eaten noodles intermittently. Each person in the factory is given 5 or 3 cents of rice per day. The number of places using this method is gradually increasing. According to foreign governments, food is not taxed domestically. In our country, there is a special tax on flour of 1 cent per bag, which should be reduced to maintain the people's food. In addition, it is more appropriate to promote wheat planting and regulate transportation. The country's wealth and the people's strength depend on this. Municipal Government Relief
